  Q2: Which students are active members of clubs?
  Q3: Which students are officers in clubs?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which students are active officers in clubs?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 36 | empty: False
   columns: ['student_id', 'student_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT s.student_id, s.student_name FROM students s JOIN memberships m ON s.student_id = m.student_id JOIN clubs c ON m.club_id = c.club_id WHERE m.active = 'yes' AND m.role = 'officer'
Q2. Which students are active members of clubs?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 84 | empty: False
   columns: ['student_id', 'student_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT s.student_id, s.student_name FROM students s JOIN memberships m ON s.student_id = m.student_id WHERE m.active = 'yes'
Q3. Which students are officers in clubs?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 45 | empty: False
   columns: ['student_id', 'student_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT s.student_id, s.student_name FROM students s JOIN memberships m ON s.student_id = m.student_id WHERE m.role = 'officer'
Q4. Which students are active presidents in clubs?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 36 | empty: False
   columns: ['student_id', 'student_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT "students"."student_id", "students"."student_name" FROM "memberships" INNER JOIN "clubs" ON "memberships"."club_id" = "clubs"."club_id" INNER JOIN "students" ON "memberships"."student_id" = "students"."student_id" WHERE "memberships"."active" = ? AND "memberships"."role" = ?

Q1. Which clubs have active president memberships?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 12 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs JOIN memberships ON memberships.club_id = clubs.club_id WHERE memberships.role = 'president' AND memberships.active = 'yes' GROUP BY clubs.club_id
Q2. Which clubs have active officer memberships?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 12 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN memberships m ON c.club_id = m.club_id WHERE m.role = 'officer' AND m.active = 'yes' GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(*) > 0
Q3. Which clubs have active memberships?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 15 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs JOIN memberships ON memberships.club_id = clubs.club_id WHERE memberships.active = 'yes' GROUP BY clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name
Q4. Which clubs have inactive memberships?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 6 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN memberships m ON c.club_id = m.club_id GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING SUM(CASE WHEN m.active = 'no' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0

Expected note: Higher capacity thresholds should be contained in lower thresholds. Workshop+capacity should be contained in all clubs hosting capacity>100 events.
Elapsed seconds: 57.15
success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True
limitations: Live-database check only. Not-contained and incomparable results are backed by counterexample rows. Contained/equivalent results are only verified on the current database, not as full symbolic proofs.

  Q2: Which clubs hosted events with capacity greater than 100?
  Q3: Which clubs hosted events with capacity greater than 50?

   success: True | safe: True | rows: 0 | empty: True

====================================================================================================
TEST 14: Attendance by event entity with feedback/stay filters
====================================================================================================
Expected note: Feedback >4 should be contained in feedback >3 and any attendance. Stayed>90 may be incomparable with feedback thresholds.
Elapsed seconds: 49.56
success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True
limitations: Live-database check only. Not-contained and incomparable results are backed by counterexample rows. Contained/equivalent results are only verified on the current database, not as full symbolic proofs.

INPUT QUERIES
  Q1: Which events had attendees with feedback score greater than 4?
  Q2: Which events had attendees with feedback score greater than 3?
  Q3: Which events had attendees who stayed more than 90 minutes?
  Q4: Which events had any attendance?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which events had attendees with feedback score greater than 4?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 42 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT events.event_id, events.event_name FROM events JOIN attendance ON attendance.event_id = events.event_id GROUP BY events.event_id HAVING MAX(attendance.feedback_score) > 4
Q2. Which events had attendees with feedback score greater than 3?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 18 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN attendance a ON e.event_id = a.event_id GROUP BY e.event_id, e.event_name HAVING AVG(a.feedback_score) > 3
Q3. Which events had attendees who stayed more than 90 minutes?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 45 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN attendance a ON e.event_id = a.event_id WHERE a.stayed_minutes > 90
Q4. Which events had any attendance?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 60 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN attendance a ON e.event_id = a.event_id

  Q3: Which events had expenses greater than 200?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which events had reimbursed expenses greater than 200?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 15 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id WHERE ee.reimbursed = 'yes' AND ee.amount > 200 GROUP BY e.event_id, e.event_name HAVING SUM(ee.amount) > 200
Q2. Which events had reimbursed expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 15 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id WHERE ee.reimbursed = 'yes'
Q3. Which events had expenses greater than 200?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 30 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id GROUP BY e.event_id, e.event_name HAVING SUM(ee.amount) > 200
Q4. Which events had any expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 30 | empty: False
   columns: ['event_id', 'event_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT e.event_id, e.event_name FROM events e JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id

====================================================================================================

Elapsed seconds: 49.65
success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True

INPUT QUERIES
  Q1: Which clubs had events with approved vendors for expenses?
  Q2: Which clubs had events with vendors for expenses?
  Q3: Which clubs had events with reimbursed expenses?
  Q4: Which clubs had any event expenses?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which clubs had events with approved vendors for expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs JOIN events ON events.club_id = clubs.club_id JOIN event_expenses ON event_expenses.event_id = events.event_id JOIN vendors ON event_expenses.vendor_id = vendors.vendor_id WHERE vendors.approved = 'yes' GROUP BY clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name
Q2. Which clubs had events with vendors for expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(ee.expense_id) > 0
Q3. Which clubs had events with reimbursed expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id WHERE ee.reimbursed = 'yes' GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name
Q4. Which clubs had any event expenses?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id JOIN event_expenses ee ON e.event_id = ee.event_id GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(ee.expense_id) > 0

success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which clubs have equipment loans with missing part condition on return?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN equipment_loans el ON c.club_id = el.club_id WHERE el.condition_on_return = 'missing_part'
Q2. Which clubs have equipment loans that were returned with any condition?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN equipment_loans el ON c.club_id = el.club_id WHERE el.condition_on_return IS NOT NULL
Q3. Which clubs have equipment loans?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN equipment_loans el ON c.club_id = el.club_id GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(*) > 0
Q4. Which clubs have equipment loans that have not been returned?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN equipment_loans el ON c.club_id = el.club_id WHERE el.return_date IS NULL GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(*) > 0

TEST 22: Cross-table students: active membership plus attendance
====================================================================================================
Expected note: Active-member attendees should be contained in active members and attended students. Inactive-member attendees may be incomparable with active-member attendees.
Elapsed seconds: 53.19
success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True
limitations: Live-database check only. Not-contained and incomparable results are backed by counterexample rows. Contained/equivalent results are only verified on the current database, not as full symbolic proofs.

INPUT QUERIES
  Q1: Which students are active club members and attended events?
  Q2: Which students are active club members?
  Q3: Which students attended events?
  Q4: Which students are inactive club members and attended events?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which students are active club members and attended events?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 83 | empty: False
   columns: ['student_id', 'student_name']
   sql: SELECT DISTINCT s.student_id, s.student_name FROM students s JOIN memberships m ON s.student_id = m.student_id JOIN attendance a ON s.student_id = a.student_id JOIN events e ON a.event_id = e.event_id JOIN clubs c ON e.club_id = c.club_id WHERE m.active = 'yes'
Q2. Which students are active club members?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 84 | empty: False

Q1. Which clubs have active members and hosted events with food provided?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN memberships m ON c.club_id = m.club_id JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id WHERE m.active = 'yes'   AND e.food_provided = 'yes' GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name
Q2. Which clubs have active members and hosted events?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN memberships m ON c.club_id = m.club_id JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id WHERE m.active = 'yes' GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT m.membership_id) > 0 AND COUNT(DISTINCT e.event_id) > 0
Q3. Which clubs hosted events with food provided?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs JOIN events ON events.club_id = clubs.club_id WHERE events.food_provided = 'yes' GROUP BY clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name
Q4. Which clubs have active members?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 15 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN memberships m ON c.club_id = m.club_id WHERE m.active = 'yes' GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(*) > 0

====================================================================================================
TEST 25: Mixed club filters: budget, events, and equipment
====================================================================================================
Expected note: Budget+events should be contained in budget-only and event-hosting clubs. Budget+equipment should be contained in budget-only and equipment-loan clubs. The two combined queries may be incomparable.
Elapsed seconds: 59.89
success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True
limitations: Live-database check only. Not-contained and incomparable results are backed by counterexample rows. Contained/equivalent results are only verified on the current database, not as full symbolic proofs.

INPUT QUERIES
  Q1: Which clubs have a budget greater than 3000 and hosted events?
  Q2: Which clubs have a budget greater than 3000?
  Q3: Which clubs hosted events?
  Q4: Which clubs have equipment loans and a budget greater than 3000?
  Q5: Which clubs have equipment loans?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which clubs have a budget greater than 3000 and hosted events?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 2 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id WHERE c.budget > 3000 GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(e.event_id) >= 1
Q2. Which clubs have a budget greater than 3000?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 8 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs WHERE clubs.budget > 3000
Q3. Which clubs hosted events?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN events e ON c.club_id = e.club_id GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(e.event_id) > 0
Q4. Which clubs have equipment loans and a budget greater than 3000?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 2 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT c.club_id, c.club_name FROM clubs c JOIN equipment_loans el ON c.club_id = el.club_id WHERE c.budget > 3000 GROUP BY c.club_id, c.club_name HAVING COUNT(el.loan_id) >= 1
Q5. Which clubs have equipment loans?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 5 | empty: False
   columns: ['club_id', 'club_name']
   sql: SELECT clubs.club_id, clubs.club_name FROM clubs JOIN equipment_loans ON clubs.club_id = equipment_loans.club_id GROUP BY clubs.club_id HAVING COUNT(*) > 0

  Q1 | status=narrower_query | empty=False | contained_in=Q2, Q3, Q5 | contains=- | equivalent_to=Q4 | incomparable_with=- | unknown_with=-
  Q2 | status=broader_query_for_some_queries | empty=False | contained_in=- | contains=Q1, Q4 | equivalent_to=- | incomparable_with=Q3, Q5 | unknown_with=-
